(Pap.); this contradiction in the early evidence is unexplained; the form <foreign lang="greek">φιδ-</foreign> or <foreign lang="greek">φειδ-</foreign> is corroborated by <bibl n="Perseus:abo:tlg,0007,004:12" default="NO"><author>Plu.</author> <title>Lyc.</title> 12</bibl>, where it is suggested that the word comes from <foreign lang="greek">φιλία</foreign> with substitution of <itype lang="greek" opt="n">δ</itype> for <itype lang="greek" opt="n">λ</itype>, or from <foreign lang="greek">φειδώ,</foreign> or from <foreign lang="greek">*ἐδίτια</foreign> (‘eatings’, cf. <foreign lang="greek">ἐδωδή</foreign>) with prefixed <foreign lang="greek">φ.</foreign> Codd. have <foreign lang="greek">φιδίτια</foreign> (or <itype lang="greek" opt="n">ον</itype>) in <author>Arist.</author> <title>Pol.</title> (v.l. φιλίτια), <author>Plu.</author> (exc. <foreign lang="greek">φιτιδίοις</foreign> <abbr>v.</abbr> l. in <title>Cleom.</title> l.c., <foreign lang="greek">φιλιτίων</foreign> all codd. in <title>Phoc.</title> l.c., <foreign lang="greek">φιλίτια</foreign> all codd. in <bibl n="Perseus:abo:tlg,0007,112:714b">2.714b</bibl>, <foreign lang="greek">φιλέστιον</foreign> in <bibl n="Perseus:abo:tlg,0007,112:697e">2.697e</bibl>), <author>Hsch.</author>; <foreign lang="greek">φειδίτια</foreign> in <author>Paus.</author>, <author>Ath.</author> (who cites <author>Antiph.</author>, <author>Dicaearch.Hist.</author>, <author>Phylarch.</author>), <author>Eust.</author>; <foreign lang="greek">φιλίτια</foreign> in <author>X.</author> (v.l. φιδίτια in <title>HG</title> l.c.), <author>Arist.</author> <title>Rh.</title> (<foreign lang="greek">φιδίτια</foreign> Sch.), <author>D.H.</author>, <author>D.Chr.</author>, <author>Philostr.</author>, <author>Them.</author>, <author>Suid.</author>; <i>philitiis</i> in <author>Cic.</author>) </sense>
